scripted_gui = {

	TMM_golmud_open = {
		context_type = player_context
		parent_window_token = politics_tab
		window_name = "TMM_golmud_menu_open"

		visible = {
			tag = QIN
			has_country_flag = battle_for_golmud_starts
		}

		effects = {
			QIN_golmud_open_button_click = {
				if = {
	   				limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = QIN_golmud_open }
	   				}
	    			set_country_flag = QIN_golmud_open
	    		}
	   			else_if = {
		   			limit = {
		      			has_country_flag = QIN_golmud_open
		   			}
					clr_country_flag = QIN_golmud_open
				}
				clr_country_flag = gui_alert_visible
			}
		}
        triggers = {
            gui_alert_visible = {
			    has_country_flag = gui_alert_visible
            }
        }
	}

	TMM_golmud_vp_menu_open = {
		context_type = player_context
		#parent_window_token = politics_tab
		window_name = "TMM_golmud_VP_menu"

		visible = {
			tag = QIN
			has_country_flag = QIN_VP_View
		}

		effects = {
			QIN_golmud_vp_close_button_click = {
				set_variable = { QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count = 0 }
				clr_country_flag = QIN_VP_View
			}
			QIN_golmud_vp_more_troops_button_click = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count
					value = 10
				}
				QINTroopCountMaxClamp = yes
			}
			QIN_golmud_vp_more_troops_button_small_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { VP_Token = 1 }
						check_variable = { QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count = BOG_STRENGTH_ALLIED^1 }
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count
						value = 0
					}                 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { VP_Token = 2 }
						check_variable = { QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count = BOG_STRENGTH_ALLIED^2 }
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count
						value = 0
					}   
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { VP_Token = 3 }

					add_to_variable = {
						var = QIN_BOG_Deploy_Count
						value = 0
					}   
				}
